<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Pomp and Circumstance
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Elgar,_Edward" title="Category:Elgar, Edward">Elgar, Edward</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.39
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IEE 59
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 marches
<dl><dt><ul><li>March No.1 in D major
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>Allegro, con molto fuoco – Trio. Largamente – Molto maestoso
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>March No.2 in A minor
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>Allegro molto
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>March No.3 in C minor
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>Con fuoco – Vivace – Cantabile – Grandioso – Animato
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>March No.4 in G major
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>Allegro marziale – Nobilmente – Grandioso
</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><ul><li>March No.5 in C major
</li></ul>
</dt><dd>Vivace
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1900-07, 1930
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>

<dl><dd>Liverpool Orchestra Society, Alfred Rodewald (conductor)
</dd></dl>

</p>
<dl><dd>London Symphony Orchestra, Edward Elgar (conductor)
</dd></dl>

</p>
<dl><dd>London Symphony Orchestra, Edward Elgar (conductor)
</dd></dl>
<p>1930-09-08 in London, Kingsway Hall (No.5)
</p>
<dl><dd>London Symphony Orchestra, Edward Elgar (conductor)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>

<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1902-07, 1930
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td>1. Alfred E. Rodewald<br />2. <a href="/wiki/Category:Bantock,_Granville" title="Category:Bantock, Granville">Granville Bantock</a><br />3. Ivor Atkins<br />4. George Sinclair<br />5. Percy Hull
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>28 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Early_20th_century" title="Category:Early 20th century">Early 20th century</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Orchestra (From all Marches)</i> <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dd>2 piccolos (one ad.lib.), 2 flutes, 2 oboes, English horn, 2 clarinets (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>/A), 
<dl><dd>bass clarinet (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>/A), 3 bassoons, contrabassoon
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>4 horns (F), 3 trumpets (F/B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>), 2 cornets (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>), 3 trombones, tuba<br />timpani, percussion, organ, 2 harps, strings
<dl><dd><small> triangle, bass drum, tenor drum, 2 snare drums (2nd ad. lib.),<br />cymbals, jingles, (tambourine, glockenspiel ad. lib.) </small> </div>
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
<td><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pomp_and_Circumstance_Marches" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Pomp and Circumstance Marches">Wikipedia article</a><br /><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.elgar.org/3pomp.htm">Elgar Society</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Elgar set text by A. C. Benson to the trio section from March No.1 for the <i><a href="/wiki/Coronation_Ode,_Op.44_(Elgar,_Edward)" title="Coronation Ode, Op.44 (Elgar, Edward)">Coronation Ode, Op.44</a></i> in 1902 as <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Land_of_Hope_and_Glory" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Land of Hope and Glory">"Land of Hope and Glory"</a>. Sketches for a March No.6 in G minor were completed by the English composer Anthony Payne in 2006.
</td></tr></table>
</div>
